020996,003568:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
020997,003569: 
020998,003570:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
020999,003571:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
021000,003572:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
021001,003573:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
021002,003574: 
021003,003575:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021004,003576:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
021005,003577:                                                                                                  #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
021006,003578:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
021007,003579:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021008,003580:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
021009,003581:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
021010,003582: 
021011,003583: 
021012,003584:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
021013,003585:                                                                                                  #           CAF    V/N
021014,003586:                                                                                                  #  L        TC     NVSUB
021015,003587:                                                                                                  #  L+1      RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
021016,003588:                                                                                                  #  L+2      RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
021017,003589: 
021018,003590: 
021019,003591:                                                                                                  #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
021020,003592:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021021,003593:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
021022,003594:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
021023,003595:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
021024,003596: 
021025,003597: 
021026,003598:                                                                                                  #         THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
021027,003599:                                                                                                  #           CAF    WAKEFCADR
021028,003600:                                                                                                  #           TC     NVSUBUSY
021029,003601: 
021030,003602: 
021031,003603:                                                                                                  #  .
021032,003604: 
021033,003605: 
021034,003606:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
021035,003607:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
021036,003608:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
021037,003609:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
021038,003610: 
021039,003611: 
021040,003612:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021041,003613:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
021042,003614:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
021043,003615:                                                                                                  #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
021044,003616:                                                                                                  #     IS EXCEEDED.
021045,003617:                                                                                                  #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 477 

021047,003619:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
021048,003620: 
021049,003621:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
021050,003622:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF(LOC
021051,003623:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
021052,003624:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
021053,003625:    4443           10604                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
021054,003626:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
021055,003627: 
021056,003628:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
021057,003629:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
021058,003630: 
021059,003631: 04,2604                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
021060,003632: 04,2604                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
021061,003633: 04,2604           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
021062,003634: 04,2605           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
021063,003635: 04,2606           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
021064,003636: 04,2607           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
021065,003637: 04,2610           30001                           CA       L                                     
021066,003638: 04,2611           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
021067,003639: 04,2612           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
021068,003640: 
021069,003641: 
021070,003642:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
021071,003643:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
021072,003644:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
021073,003645:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
021074,003646:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
021075,003647: 
021076,003648:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
021077,003649:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
021078,003650:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
021079,003651:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
021080,003652:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
021081,003653:    4450           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
021082,003654:    4451           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
021083,003655:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
021084,003656:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
021085,003657:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
021086,003658:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
021087,003659:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
021088,003660:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
021089,003661: 
021090,003662: 
021091,003663:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
021092,003664:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
021093,003665:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
021094,003666:    4457           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT
021095,003667:    4460           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
021096,003668:    4461           44736                           CS       BIT14

Page 478

021242,003814:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
021243,003815:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
021244,003816:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
021245,003817:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
021246,003818:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY,RESTART.
021247,003819:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
021248,003820:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
